<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> shaw (7136)</h1><br></body> 
***shawl.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:shawl.html>shawl</a> (40192)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Persian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Persian language">Persian</a></span> <i class="fa-Arab mention" lang="fa">شال</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="fa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">šâl</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; see there for more.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<div class="sister-wikipedia sister-project noprint floatright" style="border: 1px solid aaa; font-size: 90%; background: f9f9f9; width: 250px; padding: 4px; text-align: left;"><div style="float: left;"><div class="floatnone"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/44px-Wikipedia-logo.png" decoding="async" width="44" height="44" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/66px-Wikipedia-logo.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/88px-Wikipedia-logo.png 2x" data-file-width="200" data-file-height="200" /></div></div><div style="margin-left: 60px;">English Wikipedia <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> an article on:<div style="margin-left: 10px;"><b class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/shawl" class="extiw" title="w:shawl"><a href = vnd.unilang:shawl.html>shawl</a></a></b></div></div><span class="interProject"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/shawl" class="extiw" title="w:shawl">Wikipedia </a></span></div>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:shawl.html>shawl</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">shawls</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A square or rectangular piece of cloth worn as a covering for the head, neck, and <a href = vnd.unilang:shoulders.html>shoulders</a>, typically by women. <span class="defdate">[from 1662]</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">She wears her <b><a href = vnd.unilang:shawl.html>shawl</a></b> when it's cold outside.</i></div></dd></dl>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1898</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Winston_Churchill_(novelist)" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Winston Churchill (novelist)">Winston Churchill</a>,  chapter 5, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Celebrity" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:The Celebrity">The Celebrity</a></cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Then <a href = vnd.unilang:came.html>came</a> a maid with hand-bag and <b>shawls</b>, and after her a tall young lady. She stood for a <a href = vnd.unilang:moment.html>moment</a> holding her skirt above the grimy <a href = vnd.unilang:steps.html>steps</a>,<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span>, and the light of the reflector fell full upon her.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1967</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Barbara_Sleigh" class="extiw" title="w:Barbara Sleigh">Sleigh, Barbara</a>,  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Jessamy" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Jessamy">Jessamy</a></cite>, 1993 edition, Sevenoaks, <a href = vnd.unilang:kent.html>Kent</a> |  Bloomsbury, <small>→ISBN</small>, page 26:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Jessamy <a href = vnd.unilang:turned.html>turned</a>. Her uplifted candle showed a dark handsome young women in a black dress. She wore a wide <b><a href = vnd.unilang:shawl.html>shawl</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> her head which hung down on either side, only partially hiding a starched, white apron..</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>A fold of wrinkled flesh under the <a href = vnd.unilang:lips.html>lips</a> and neck of a bloodhound, used in scenting.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">beshawled</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:shawl.html>shawl</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">shawls</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">shawling</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">shawled</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To wrap in a <a href = vnd.unilang:shawl.html>shawl</a>.
<dl><dd><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> find and add a quotation of Thackeray to this entry?)</span></dd></dl></li></ol>

***sheen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:sheen.html>sheen</a> (44668)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">shene</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:schijnen.html>schene</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">sċīene</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">beautiful, fair, bright, brilliant, light</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*skauniz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">beautiful</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*(s)kewh₁-</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scots_language" class="extiw" title="w:Scots language">Scots</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sco"><a href = vnd.unilang:schijnen.html>schene</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="sco">scheine</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">beautiful, fair, attractive</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Saterland_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Saterland Frisian language">Saterland Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="stq">skeen</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">clean, pure</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">skjin</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">nice, clean</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schoon.html>schoon</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">clean, beautiful, fair</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">schön</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">beautiful</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">skøn</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">beautiful</span><span See also <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">show</i>.

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:sheen.html>sheen</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en comparative-form-of" lang="en">sheener</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en superlative-form-of" lang="en">sheenest</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:rare.html>rare</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> poetic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Beautiful, good-looking, attractive; radiant; shiny.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1814</b>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:walter.html>Walter</a> Scott,  <cite>Waverley</cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Where the fountains glisten <b>sheenest</b> <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span> (ch. 12).</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> date this quote by Fairfax and provide title, author’s full name, and other <a href = vnd.unilang:details.html>details</a>?)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Up <a href = vnd.unilang:rose.html>rose</a> each warrier bold and <a href = vnd.unilang:brave.html>brave</a>, / Glistening in filed steel and armor <b><a href = vnd.unilang:sheen.html>sheen</a></b>.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">sheenly</span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:sheen.html>sheen</a></strong> (<i>countable and uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">sheens</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Splendor; radiance; shininess.
<ul><li><b>1946</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mervyn_Peake" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Mervyn Peake">Mervyn Peake</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Titus_Groan" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Titus Groan">Titus Groan</a></i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">There <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a greenish <b><a href = vnd.unilang:sheen.html>sheen</a></b> across the <a href = vnd.unilang:shoulders.html>shoulders</a> of his greasy black suit, for the morning light <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> of a sudden <a href = vnd.unilang:begun.html>begun</a> to dance through the bay window.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>A thin layer of a substance (such as oil) spread on a solid or liquid surface.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">oil <b><a href = vnd.unilang:sheen.html>sheen</a></b></i></div></dd></dl>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2004</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harold_McGee" class="extiw" title="w:Harold McGee">Harold McGee</a>,  chapter 1, in  <cite>On Food and Cooking: The Science and Lore of the Kitchen</cite>, <small>→ISBN</small>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Perhaps the simplest of sauces <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> the pat of butter dropped on a heap of hot vegetables, or stirred into rice or <a href = vnd.unilang:noodles.html>noodles</a>, or drawn across the surface of an <a href = vnd.unilang:omelet.html>omelet</a> or <a href = vnd.unilang:steak.html>steak</a> to give a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:sheen.html>sheen</a></b>.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><b>2017</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:jeffrey.html>Jeffrey</a> Miller, Ann Powers, <i>Introduction to Environmental Law: <a href = vnd.unilang:cases.html>Cases</a> and Materials on Water Pollution Control</i>, West Academic (→ISBN)
<dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Take the floating scum or oil <b><a href = vnd.unilang:sheen.html>sheen</a></b> prohibitions. A discharger or an inspector simply can look to see if scum, or an oil <b><a href = vnd.unilang:sheen.html>sheen</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> coming from a particular  discharge. Assume an oil <b><a href = vnd.unilang:sheen.html>sheen</a></b> begins at a discharge—is the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:sheen.html>sheen</a></b> caused by that <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span></span></div></dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms_2">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">sheenless</span></li>

***sherpa.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:sherpa.html>sherpa</a> (63038)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:sherpa.html>Sherpa</a></i>. The verb derives from the noun.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:sherpa.html>sherpa</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">sherpas</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A mountain guide or <a href = vnd.unilang:porter.html>porter</a>, particularly a male of the <a href = vnd.unilang:sherpa.html>Sherpa</a> people so employed.</li>
<li>An expert sent by a country’s leader to a summit meeting.</li>
<li>A synthetic fabric with a long, thick pile, similar to faux fur, imitation lamb wool<span class="serial-comma">,</span> or fleece.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:sherpa.html>sherpa</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">sherpas</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">sherpaing</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">sherpaed</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:rare.html>rare</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To serve as a guide or <a href = vnd.unilang:porter.html>porter</a> for another.</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:sherpa.html>sherpa</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>

***shirt.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:shirt.html>shirt</a> (2593)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">sherte</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">shurte</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">schirte</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">sċyrte</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a short garment; skirt; kirtle</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*skurtijǭ</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schort.html>schort</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Schürze</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">apron</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Norwegian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Norwegian language">Norwegian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="no">skjorte</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:shirt.html>shirt</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Faroese_language" class="extiw" title="w:Faroese language">Faroese</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fo">skjúrta</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:shirt.html>shirt</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">Skirt</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a parallel formation from Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a>; which <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">short</i>, from the same ultimate source.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:shirt.html>shirt</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:shirts.html>shirts</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>An article of clothing that <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> worn on the upper part of the body, and often <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> sleeves, either long or short, that cover the arms.
<ul><li><b>1705</b> (revised <b>1718</b>), <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Joseph_Addison" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Joseph Addison">Joseph Addison</a>, <i>Remarks on Several Parts of Italy</i>
<dl><dd>Several persons in December <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> nothing <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> their <a href = vnd.unilang:shoulders.html>shoulders</a> but their <b><a href = vnd.unilang:shirts.html>shirts</a></b>.</dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> date this quote by Bishop Fisher and provide title, author's full name, and other <a href = vnd.unilang:details.html>details</a>?)</span>
<dl><dd>She <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> her <b><a href = vnd.unilang:shirts.html>shirts</a></b> and girdles of hair.</dd></dl></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2012</b> April 9,  Mandeep Sanghera,  “Tottenham 1 <a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a> 2 Norwich”, in  <cite>BBC Sport</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/sport/0/football/17581358">[1]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Holt <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> furious referee Michael <a href = vnd.unilang:oliver.html>Oliver</a> refused to then award him a penalty after Ledley King appeared to pull his <b><a href = vnd.unilang:shirt.html>shirt</a></b> and his anger <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> compounded when <a href = vnd.unilang:spurs.html>Spurs</a> immediately levelled.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>An interior lining in a blast furnace.</li>
<li>A member of the shirt-wearing team in a <a href = vnd.unilang:shirts.html>shirts</a> and <a href = vnd.unilang:skins.html>skins</a> game.</li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">sherten</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">shirten</i> (also <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">shorten</i>), from the noun (see above).
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:shirt.html>shirt</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:shirts.html>shirts</a></b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">shirting</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">shirted</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>To cover or clothe with a <a href = vnd.unilang:shirt.html>shirt</a>, or as if with a <a href = vnd.unilang:shirt.html>shirt</a>.
<ul><li><b>1691,</b> <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/King_Arthur_(opera)" class="extiw" title="w:King Arthur (opera)">King Arthur</a>,</i> by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/John_Dryden" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:John Dryden">John Dryden</a>, act II, scene I.
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:ah.html>Ah</a>! for so many <a href = vnd.unilang:souls.html>souls</a>, as but this <a href = vnd.unilang:morn.html>morn</a> / <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>Were</a> clothed with flesh, and <a href = vnd.unilang:warm.html>warm</a>’d with vital blood / But naked now, or <b>shirted</b> just with air.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>

***shoemaker.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:shoemaker.html>shoemaker</a> (30939)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">scho makere</i>, equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">shoe</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">maker</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schoenmaker.html>schoenmaker</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Schuhmacher</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">skomager</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:shoemaker.html>shoemaker</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">shoemakers</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A person who <a href = vnd.unilang:makes.html>makes</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:shoes.html>shoes</a></li>
<li>The threadfish.</li>
<li>A fish, <span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Elagatis_pinnulatis" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Elagatis pinnulatis"><i>Elagatis pinnulatis</i></a></span>, the runner.</li></ol>
<div style="background-color: f0f0f0;">
<p><i>Part or all of this entry <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> imported from the 1913 edition of </i>Webster’s Dictionary<i>, which <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> now free of copyright and hence in the public domain. The imported definitions may be significantly out of date, and any more recent senses may be completely missing.<br />(See the entry for <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.websters1913.com/words/Shoemaker"><a href = vnd.unilang:shoemaker.html>shoemaker</a></a> in </i>Webster’s Revised Unabridged Dictionary<i>, G. amp; C. Merriam, 1913.)</i>

***shoo.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:shoo.html>shoo</a> (40187)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schuwen.html>schuwen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to shun</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">scheuchen</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to scare, drive away</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:shoo.html>shoo</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">shoos</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">shooing</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">shooed</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To induce someone or something to leave.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">Don'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> just <b><a href = vnd.unilang:shoo.html>shoo</a></b> away mosquitoes, kill them!</i></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">See if you can <b><a href = vnd.unilang:shoo.html>shoo</a></b> off the insurance salesmen.</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To leave under inducement.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">You kids <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> better <b><a href = vnd.unilang:shoo.html>shoo</a></b> before your parents get a call.</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:rare.html>rare</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To usher someone.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:shoo.html>Shoo</a></b> the visitor in.</i></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> shooting (5454)</h1><br><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>

***shrike.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:shrike.html>shrike</a> (63028)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">*schrike</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">*schryke</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">sċrīc</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:shrike.html>shrike</a>, thrush</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from the same root as <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">shriek</i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:screech.html>screech</a></i>, named after the bird's cry. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Icelandic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Icelandic language">Icelandic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="is">skríkja</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">shrieker, <a href = vnd.unilang:shrike.html>shrike</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">skrika</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:jay.html>jay</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<div class="sister-wikipedia sister-project noprint floatright" style="border: 1px solid aaa; font-size: 90%; background: f9f9f9; width: 250px; padding: 4px; text-align: left;"><div style="float: left;"><div class="floatnone"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/44px-Wikipedia-logo.png" decoding="async" width="44" height="44" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/66px-Wikipedia-logo.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/88px-Wikipedia-logo.png 2x" data-file-width="200" data-file-height="200" /></div></div><div style="margin-left: 60px;">English Wikipedia <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> an article on:<div style="margin-left: 10px;"><b class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/shrike" class="extiw" title="w:shrike"><a href = vnd.unilang:shrike.html>shrike</a></a></b></div></div><span class="interProject"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/shrike" class="extiw" title="w:shrike">Wikipedia </a></span></div>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:shrike.html>shrike</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">shrikes</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Any of various passerine <a href = vnd.unilang:birds.html>birds</a> of the family Laniidae which are known for their habit of catching other <a href = vnd.unilang:birds.html>birds</a> and small animals and impaling the uneaten portions of their <a href = vnd.unilang:bodies.html>bodies</a> on thorns.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">butcherbird</span></li></ul>

<li><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/shrike_thrush" class="extiw" title="w:shrike thrush"><a href = vnd.unilang:shrike.html>shrike</a> thrush</a></li>

</body>

***shylock.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:shylock.html>shylock</a> (37756)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From the character <a href = vnd.unilang:shylock.html>Shylock</a> in Shakespeare's <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Merchant_of_Venice" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:The Merchant of Venice">The Merchant of Venice</a></i> (1600).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:shylock.html>shylock</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">shylocks</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_States" class="extiw" title="w:United States">US</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A loan shark; a usurer.
<ul><li><b>2005</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:joe.html>Joe</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:pistone.html>Pistone</a>, <i>The Way of the Wiseguy</i>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://books.google.com.au/books?id=L62GGItma-QCamp;pg=PA45amp;dq=%22shylocks%22amp;hl=enamp;sa=Xamp;ei=D1mAU6fAFoyOlQXp9YHYBAamp;ved=0CL8BEOgBMBwv=onepageamp;q=%22shylocks%22amp;f=false">page 45</a>,
<dl><dd>Eventually, their gambling debts grow so big that they are cut off from making any more bets, eliminating the chance that they can make enough money to satisfy their <b>shylocks</b>.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>2009</b>, G. <a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>T</a>. Harrell, <i>For Members Only: The Story of the Mob's Secret Judge, A True Story</i>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://books.google.com.au/books?id=TtdrM32cVnMCamp;pg=PA229amp;dq=%22shylocks%22amp;hl=enamp;sa=Xamp;ei=D1mAU6fAFoyOlQXp9YHYBAamp;ved=0CDsQ6AEwAwv=onepageamp;q=%22shylocks%22amp;f=false">page 229</a>,
<dl><dd>If a guy got into hock with several <b>shylocks</b> from different <a href = vnd.unilang:crews.html>crews</a> and <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> unable to keep up with his weekly payments, a sit-down would have to be called with all of the <b>shylocks</b> involved and their respective capos.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>2013</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/James_Lee_Burke" class="extiw" title="w:James Lee Burke">James Lee <a href = vnd.unilang:burke.html>Burke</a></a>, <i>Light of the World</i>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://books.google.com.au/books?id=yXwVAAAAQBAJamp;pg=PA429amp;dq=%22shylocks%22amp;hl=enamp;sa=Xamp;ei=D1mAU6fAFoyOlQXp9YHYBAamp;ved=0CK0BEOgBMBkv=onepageamp;q=%22shylocks%22amp;f=false">page 429</a>,
<dl><dd>After Caspian's father killed his credit lines at all the big casinos, he <a href = vnd.unilang:ran.html>ran</a> up a six-figure tab with a couple of <b>shylocks</b> in Miami, then couldn'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> make the <a href = vnd.unilang:vig.html>vig</a>.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">offensive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> ethnic slur</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A person of Jewish descent.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">Yid</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">not always pejorative</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:heeb.html>heeb</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:hymie.html>hymie</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">kike</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">sheeny</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:shylock.html>shylock</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">shylocks</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">shylocking</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">shylocked</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_States" class="extiw" title="w:United States">US</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To lend money at <a href = vnd.unilang:exorbitant.html>exorbitant</a> rates of interest.
<ul><li><b>2004</b> December 8, <i>Kenya National Assembly Official Record (Hansard)</i>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://books.google.com.au/books?id=08uRz2b2TecCamp;pg=PT23amp;dq=%22shylocking%22%7C%22shylocked%22amp;hl=enamp;sa=Xamp;ei=PVSAU-2-CcanlAX3xIGYBgamp;redir_esc=yv=onepageamp;q=%22shylocking%22%7C%22shylocked%22amp;f=false">page 4928</a>,
<dl><dd>I <a href = vnd.unilang:wanted.html>wanted</a> to know whether <b>shylocking</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a legal business or not, and if it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> legal, under which Act does it operate?</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>2005</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:tom.html>Tom</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:layne.html>Layne</a>, <i>The Assassination of Rush Limbaugh</i>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://books.google.com.au/books?id=dh0ifYkfgw8Camp;pg=PA151amp;dq=%22shylocking%22%7C%22shylocked%22amp;hl=enamp;sa=Xamp;ei=PVSAU-2-CcanlAX3xIGYBgamp;redir_esc=yv=onepageamp;q=%22shylocking%22%7C%22shylocked%22amp;f=false">page 151</a>,
<dl><dd>When you've accumulated a good stash of money, you may want to go into the nightclub business, or <b>shylocking</b>. <b>Shylocking</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> free. There <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> no ten percent <a href = vnd.unilang:vig.html>vig</a> on loan sharking.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>2005</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Jeannette_Walls" class="extiw" title="w:Jeannette Walls"><a href = vnd.unilang:jeannette.html>Jeannette</a> Walls</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Glass_Castle" class="extiw" title="w:The Glass Castle">The Glass Castle</a></i>, 2010, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://books.google.com.au/books?id=opdvCefTFngCamp;pg=PT93amp;dq=%22shylocking%22%7C%22shylocked%22amp;hl=enamp;sa=Xamp;ei=PVSAU-2-CcanlAX3xIGYBgamp;redir_esc=yv=onepageamp;q=%22shylocking%22%7C%22shylocked%22amp;f=false">unnumbered page</a>,
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:lori.html>Lori</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:said.html>said</a> it sounded outright felonious, but Dad <a href = vnd.unilang:said.html>said</a> all he <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> doing <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> outsmarting the fat-cat bank owners who <b>shylocked</b> the common <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a> by charging usurious interest rates.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>2011</b>, John Nicholas Iannuzzi, <i>Handbook of Cross Examination: The Mosaic Art</i>, 3rd Edition, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://books.google.com.au/books?id=Z1X9biJmRcQCamp;pg=PA312amp;dq=%22shylocking%22%7C%22shylocked%22amp;hl=enamp;sa=Xamp;ei=PVSAU-2-CcanlAX3xIGYBgamp;redir_esc=yv=onepageamp;q=%22shylocking%22%7C%22shylocked%22amp;f=false">page 312</a>,
<dl><dd>Do you recall this question having <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> put to you—the <b>shylocking</b> business you <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> involved in continued right up until the time that you <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> arrested, correct?</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>

<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">side</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">car</i>

***sieren.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:sieren.html>sieren</a> (59232)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">cieren</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">tsieren</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:sieren.html>sieren</a></i>, borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">zieren</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">zieren</i> and the inherited form <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tieren.html>tieren</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:sieren.html>sieren</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to adorn, to decorate</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to befit, to be appropriate for
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> boetekleed <b><a href = vnd.unilang:siert.html>siert</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mens.html>mens</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">It <b><a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> appropriate for</b> a human to do penance for wrongdoing.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be nice of, to be decent of
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>Dat</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:siert.html>siert</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:u.html>u</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">That <b><a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> nice of</b> you.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
